Generally speaking, although the hotel has a good location, the service is okay, and there are many complimentary services, it feels like the hotel wants to do a good job, but the control of details still needs to be further improved before it can be further aligned with five stars.

The breakfast is also quite rich, and the noodles taste very good, and there is no charge for children who are actually over 1.2 meters. The beautiful lady Liao from the room management met us in the elevator and asked us if we had sand digging tools. When she knew we didn't have one, she sent a set to the room for us. Although the hotel's two swimming pools are not very big, one is an infinity pool and the other is a children's pool, the children still like it very much. There is a bubble machine spraying foam in the children's pool on the third floor on the second day of check-in. The children played for three hours. There are parent-child activities in Beiye every morning and afternoon. Children also like it very much. They participated in archery, tug-of-war, coloring masks, and baking. Guoguo, Hengde, and Teacher Kongkong are all very responsible and caring. Before leaving, there was a photo frame made by Teacher Guoguo and a printed photo of the child. Of course, due to government construction, there is still a bit of noise during the day, and the Rainbow Bridge cannot be used because of this. To go to the beach, you still have to make a detour. In general, although the hotel is not big, it is very warm and comfortable to live in. I will come again next time I have a chance to bring my children.
